   Then - {Set} {Request ID} = {Specimen ID}

Rule # 4
   Desc - A.1 - Rule to Block a3600 Queue Error
   Child of Rule # 3 - Then

   Then - {Set} {Result} {On That Test} = "XXX" {AND} {Set} {Test Comment(s)} {On That Test} = "a3600 Contaminated Sample Risk-Automation Movement Error, Redraw Sample" {AND} {Hold That Test for Verification}

Rule # 5
   Desc - A.2 - Rule to set results to EXCEPTION
   Child of Rule # 3 - Then
   If - {Any} {Error Code(s)} {On Any Test} {Contains} "Exception"

Rule # 6
   Desc - A.3 - Rule for Error 8070
   Child of Rule # 3 - Then

Rule # 21
   Desc - 0.0.4 - HBS CONF %N = Exception Add HBS CONF
   Child of Rule # 17 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF_%N" ) {AND} ( {NOT} {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF_%N" = "EXCEPTION" )
   Then - {Add Test} "HBS CONF" {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "EXCEPTION" {AND} {Set} {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF_%N" {AND} {Set} {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "HBS CONF_%N"

Rule # 22
   Desc - 0.0.5 - Set Test Dilution on HBS CONF = HBS CONF_%N
   Child of Rule # 17 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF_%N" ) {AND} ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" {NOT} = {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF_%N" )

   Then - {Set} {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "," {Concatenated With} {Value List:ErrorName} {AND} {Order Test} {Value List:TestCode2} {AND} {Order Test} {Value List:TestCode3} {AND} {Set} {VMT RERUN Marker} = ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Concatenated With} ( {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive," ) )
   Use Parent's Value List - Yes

Rule # 268
   Desc - 7.5.3.1 - Invalid NEAT Rerun
   Child of Rule # 267 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Invalid" ) {AND} ( ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "UNDILUTED" ) ) {AND} ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" )
   Then - {Rerun Test} "HBS CONF" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "INVALIDRERUNNEAT" {AND} {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"

Rule # 269
   Desc - 7.5.3.2 - Inconclusive NEAT Order 1:500 Dilution
   Child of Rule # 267 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Inconclusive" ) {AND} ( ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "UNDILUTED" ) ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "INVALIDRERUNNEAT" ) )
   Then - {Rerun Test} "HBS CONF" {With Test Dilution} "1:500" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "DILUTION1" {AND} {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"

Rule # 275
   Desc - 9.1 - Add ALT and Set Result = E if >=110
   Child of Rule # 274 - Then
   If - ( ( ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" > = "110" ) ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Contains} ">" ) ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "CRITCONF" ) )
   Then - {Add Test} "ALT" {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} "ALT" = "E" {AND} {Set} {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "ALT" = {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALTIU"
   Comment - This rule checks to see if the result on ALT IU is numeric and if it is >= 110. If so, ALT is added and the result is set to E.

   Comment - This rule checks to see if the result on ALT IU is numeric and if it is <=109. If so, ALT is added and the result is set to E.

Rule # 302
   Desc - 11.3.2 - Sorting After On-Track Testing is Complete
   Child of Rule # 300 - Then
   If - {Always}

Rule # 303
   Desc - 11.3.2.1 - CHOL, not FER,AHIV
   Child of Rule # 302 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "CHOL" ) {AND} ( {Starlims Orders} {NOT} {Contains} ",HIV" ) {AND} ( {Starlims Orders} {Contains} ",CHOL" ) {AND} ( {Starlims Orders} {NOT} {Contains} ",FER" ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "CHOL" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "CHOL" = "CRITCONF" ) )
   Then - {Order Test} "CHOLSORT"

Rule # 304
   Desc - 11.3.2.2 - ALTIU not HBT
   Child of Rule # 302 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "ALTIU" ) {AND} ( {Starlims Orders} {NOT} {Contains} ",HBT" ) {AND} ( {Starlims Orders} {Contains} ",ALTIU" ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "CRITCONF" ) )
   Then - {Order Test} "ALTSORT"

Rule # 305
   Desc - 11.3.2.3 - HBT not ALTIU
   Child of Rule # 302 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBT" ) {AND} ( {Starlims Orders} {Contains} ",HBT" ) {AND} ( {Starlims Orders} {NOT} {Contains} ",ALTIU" ) {AND} ( {Alinity VMT Valid Result Counter} {Contains} "HBTF" )
   Then - {Order Test} "HBTSORT"

Rule # 306
   Desc - 11.3.3 - Repeat Reactive AHIV, AHTLV, AHCV, ACHAG, AHBS Order Sort Test
   Child of Rule # 300 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} {Value List:TestCodeF} ) {AND} ( {Final?} {On Test} {Value List:TestCodeF} {Contains} "FINAL" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCodeF} = "Reactive" )
   Then - {Order Test} {Value List:RepeatReactiveSort}

   Desc - 11.4.1.1 - HIV,CHOL not FER
   Child of Rule # 309 - Then

   Then - {Order Test} "VMT5"

Rule # 311
   Desc - 11.4.1.2 - HIV,FER not CHOL
   Child of Rule # 309 - Then

   Desc - 11.4.1.3 - HIV,FER,CHOL

   Then - {Order Test} "VMT5"

Rule # 319
   Desc - Step 12 - LIS Formatting
   Child of Rule # 1 - Then
   If - {Always}

Rule # 320
   Desc - 12.1 - Round TET > 99.99 to 0 Decimal Places
   Child of Rule # 319 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "TET" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "TET" > "99.99" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "TET" {Is Numeric} )
   Then - {Round} {Result} {On Test} "TET" {To} "0" {Decimal Places}

Rule # 321
   Desc - 12.2 - Round TET > 497.00 to 0 Decimal Places
   Child of Rule # 319 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "TET" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "TET" = "> 497.00" )
   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "TET" = "> 497"

Rule # 322
   Desc - 12.3 - Set TET = 2.01 & Error Codes = Null if < 2.01
   Child of Rule # 319 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "TET" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "TET" {Contains} "<" )
   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "TET" = {Extract Section of} {Result} {On Test} "TET" {From} "3" {To} "6"

Rule # 323
   Desc - 12.4 - HBT > 25000 & Decimal Handling
   Child of Rule # 319 - Then
   If - {Always}

Rule # 324
   Desc - 12.3.1 - Round HBT > 25000.00 to 0 Decimals
   Child of Rule # 323 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBT" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" = "> 25000.00" )
   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "HBT" = "25000"

Rule # 325
   Desc - 12.3.2 - Round Numeric HBT Result to 0 Decimals
   Child of Rule # 323 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBT" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Contains} "." ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" > "0.50" )
   Then - {Round} {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {To} "0" {Decimal Places}

Rule # 326
   Desc - 12.3.3 - Set HBT <=0.50 to 1
   Child of Rule # 323 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBT" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Contains} "." ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" < = "0.50" )
   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "HBT" = "1"

   Desc - 12.9 - Set SUF09 = RERUN or Null (For Workspace Processing)
   Child of Rule # 319 - Then

   Then - {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"
   Else - {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = ""

   Then - {Set} {Interpreted Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = "INV Dilution" {AND} {Set} {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "INVALID DILUTION"
   Use Parent's Value List - Yes

Rule # 503
   Desc - 4.5.1.2 - Nonreactive
   Child of Rule # 501 - Then
   If - ( ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} < {Value List:TestLow} ) ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Contains} "<" )

   Use Parent's Value List - Yes

Rule # 504
   Desc - 4.5.1.3 - Reactive
   Child of Rule # 501 - Then
   If - ( ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} > = {Value List:TestLow} ) ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Contains} ">" )
   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Value List:PosResult} {AND} {Set} {Alinity VMT Interp Result Storage} = {Alinity VMT Interp Result Storage} {Concatenated With} {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "R-" {AND} {Add} {Error Name(s)} {Value List:ErrorCode} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode}
   Use Parent's Value List - Yes

Rule # 505
   Desc - 4.5.1.4 - Set Result INVALID TestCodeF Already Determined
   Child of Rule # 501 - Then

   Then - {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = "INVALID" {AND} {Set} {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} ",Final Result Already Determined" {AND} {Reject Test} {Value List:TestCode}
   Use Parent's Value List - Yes

Rule # 506
   Desc - 4.5.1.5 - Initial Nonreactive as Final

   Desc - 7.5.3 - HBS CONF Rerun & Dilution Processing
   Child of Rule # 592 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Invalid" ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Inconclusive" ) )

Rule # 619
   Desc - 7.5.3.1 - Invalid NEAT Rerun
   Child of Rule # 618 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Invalid" ) {AND} ( ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "UNDILUTED" ) ) {AND} ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" )
   Then - {Rerun Test} "HBS CONF" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "INVALIDRERUNNEAT" {AND} {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"

Rule # 620
   Desc - 7.5.3.2 - Inconclusive NEAT Order 1:500 Dilution
   Child of Rule # 618 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Inconclusive" ) {AND} ( ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "UNDILUTED" ) ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "INVALIDRERUNNEAT" ) )
   Then - {Rerun Test} "HBS CONF" {With Test Dilution} "1:500" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "DILUTION1" {AND} {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"

Rule # 626
   Desc - 9.1 - Add ALT and Set Result = E if >=110
   Child of Rule # 625 - Then
   If - ( ( ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" > = "110" ) ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Contains} ">" ) ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "CRITCONF" ) )
   Then - {Add Test} "ALT" {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} "ALT" = "E" {AND} {Set} {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "ALT" = {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALTIU"
   Comment - This rule checks to see if the result on ALT IU is numeric and if it is >= 110. If so, ALT is added and the result is set to E.

Rule # 627
   Desc - 9.2 - Add ALT and Set Result = N if <=109
   Child of Rule # 625 - Then
   If - ( ( ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" < = "109" ) ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Contains} "<" ) ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "CRITCONF" ) )
   Then - {Add Test} "ALT" {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} "ALT" = "N" {AND} {Set} {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "ALT" = {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALTIU"
   Comment - This rule checks to see if the result on ALT IU is numeric and if it is <=109. If so, ALT is added and the result is set to E.

   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Final?} {On Test} "HBS CONF" {NOT} = "FINAL" ) {AND} ( ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Confirmed Positive" ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Not Confirmed" ) )
   Then - {Set} {Final?} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "FINAL" {AND} {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = ""

Rule # 684
   Desc - 12.8 - Add TestCode-Complete to VMT Rerun Marker
   Child of Rule # 670 - Then
   If - ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} {Value List:TestCode} ) {AND} ( {Alinity VMT Valid Result Counter} {Contains} ( {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "F" ) ) {AND} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {NOT} {Contains} ( {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "-Complete" ) )
   Then - {Set} {VMT RERUN Marker} = ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Concatenated With} {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "-Complete," )

Rule # 685
   Desc - 12.9 - Set SUF09 = RERUN or Null (For Workspace Processing)
   Child of Rule # 670 - Then
   If - ( ( ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HIV} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive" ) ) {OR} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HIV} {Concatenated With} "-Exception" ) ) ) {AND} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {NOT} {Contains} ( {Value List:HIV} {Concatenated With} "-Complete" ) ) ) {OR} ( ( ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HCV} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive" ) ) {OR} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HCV} {Concatenated With} "-Exception" ) ) ) {AND} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {NOT} {Contains} ( {Value List:HCV} {Concatenated With} "-Complete" ) ) ) {OR} ( ( ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HBS} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive" ) ) {OR} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HBS} {Concatenated With} "-Exception" ) ) ) {AND} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {NOT} {Contains} ( {Value List:HBS} {Concatenated With} "-Complete" ) ) ) {OR} ( ( ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HBC} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive" ) ) {OR} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HBC} {Concatenated With} "-Exception" ) ) ) {AND} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {NOT} {Contains} ( {Value List:HBC} {Concatenated With} "-Complete" ) ) ) {OR} ( ( ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HTLV} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive" ) ) {OR} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:HTLV} {Concatenated With} "-Exception" ) ) ) {AND} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {NOT} {Contains} ( {Value List:HTLV} {Concatenated With} "-Complete" ) ) ) {OR} ( ( ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:CHAG} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive" ) ) {OR} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Contains} ( {Value List:CHAG} {Concatenated With} "-Exception" ) ) ) {AND} ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {NOT} {Contains} ( {Value List:CHAG} {Concatenated With} "-Complete" ) ) )
   Then - {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"
   Else - {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = ""

   If - {Always}
   Protected - Yes

   Desc - A.3 - Rule for Error 8070
   Child of Rule # 1 - Then
   If - ( {Result} {On Any Test} = "EXCEPTION" ) {AND} ( {Error Code(s)} {On That Test} {Contains} "8070" )

Rule # 19
   Desc - 0.0.4 - HBS CONF %N = Exception Add HBS CONF
   Child of Rule # 15 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF_%N" ) {AND} ( {NOT} {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF_%N" = "EXCEPTION" )
   Then - {Add Test} "HBS CONF" {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "EXCEPTION" {AND} {Set} {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF_%N" {AND} {Set} {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "HBS CONF_%N"

   Then - {Set} {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Hold Test Flag} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "," {Concatenated With} {Value List:ErrorName} {AND} {Order Test} {Value List:TestCode2} {AND} {Order Test} {Value List:TestCode3} {AND} {Set} {VMT RERUN Marker} = ( {VMT RERUN Marker} {Concatenated With} ( {Value List:TestCode} {Concatenated With} "-Reactive," ) )
   Use Parent's Value List - Yes

   Desc - 7.5.3 - HBS CONF Rerun & Dilution Processing
   Child of Rule # 239 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Invalid" ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Inconclusive" ) )

Rule # 266
   Desc - 7.5.3.1 - Invalid NEAT Rerun
   Child of Rule # 265 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Invalid" ) {AND} ( ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "UNDILUTED" ) ) {AND} ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" )
   Then - {Rerun Test} "HBS CONF" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "INVALIDRERUNNEAT" {AND} {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"

Rule # 267
   Desc - 7.5.3.2 - Inconclusive NEAT Order 1:500 Dilution
   Child of Rule # 265 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBS CONF" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "Inconclusive" ) {AND} ( ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "UNDILUTED" ) ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "INVALIDRERUNNEAT" ) )
   Then - {Rerun Test} "HBS CONF" {With Test Dilution} "1:500" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "HBS CONF" = "DILUTION1" {AND} {Set} {Specimen User Field 09} = "RERUN"

Rule # 273
   Desc - 9.1 - Add ALT and Set Result = E if >=110
   Child of Rule # 272 - Then
   If - ( ( ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" > = "110" ) ) {OR} ( {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {Contains} ">" ) ) {AND} ( ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "" ) {OR} ( {Previous Test Error} {On Test} "ALTIU" = "CRITCONF" ) )
   Then - {Add Test} "ALT" {AND} {Set} {Result} {On Test} "ALT" = "E" {AND} {Set} {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Code(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALT" = {Error Name(s)} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Previous Test Dilution} {On Test} "ALT" = {Result} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Instrument ID} {On Test} "ALTIU" {AND} {Set} {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALT" = {Test Operator ID} {On Test} "ALTIU"
   Comment - This rule checks to see if the result on ALT IU is numeric and if it is >= 110. If so, ALT is added and the result is set to E.

Rule # 301
   Desc - 11.3.2.1 - CHOL, not FER,AHIV
   Child of Rule # 300 - Then

   Then - {Order Test} "CHOLSORT"

   Desc - 11.3.2.2 - ALTIU not HBT

   Desc - 11.3.2.3 - HBT not ALTIU

   Then - {Order Test} "HBTSORT"

   Desc - Step 12 - LIS Formatting
   If - {Always}

Rule # 318
   Desc - 12.1 - Round TET > 99.99 to 0 Decimal Places
   Child of Rule # 317 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "TET" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "TET" > "99.99" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "TET" {Is Numeric} )
   Then - {Round} {Result} {On Test} "TET" {To} "0" {Decimal Places}

Rule # 319
   Desc - 12.2 - Round TET > 497.00 to 0 Decimal Places
   Child of Rule # 317 - Then

   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "TET" = "> 497"

   Desc - 12.3 - Set TET = 2.01 & Error Codes = Null if < 2.01
   Child of Rule # 317 - Then

   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "TET" = {Extract Section of} {Result} {On Test} "TET" {From} "3" {To} "6"

   Desc - 12.4 - HBT > 25000 & Decimal Handling

   If - {Always}

Rule # 322
   Desc - 12.3.1 - Round HBT > 25000.00 to 0 Decimals
   Child of Rule # 321 - Then

   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "HBT" = "25000"

Rule # 323
   Desc - 12.3.2 - Round Numeric HBT Result to 0 Decimals
   Child of Rule # 321 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBT" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Contains} "." ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" > "0.50" )
   Then - {Round} {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {To} "0" {Decimal Places}

Rule # 324
   Desc - 12.3.3 - Set HBT <=0.50 to 1
   Child of Rule # 321 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} "HBT" ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Is Numeric} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" {Contains} "." ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} "HBT" < = "0.50" )
   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} "HBT" = "1"

Rule # 342
   Desc - 13.4 - Convert Abbott Result Terminology to Customer Terminology HBT/COVID
   Child of Rule # 335 - Then
   If - ( {Test Resulted} {Value List:TestCode} ) {AND} ( {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Value List:AbbottTerm} ) {AND} ( {Value List:AbbottTerm} {NOT} = {Value List:CustomerTerm} )
   Then - {Set} {Result} {On Test} {Value List:TestCode} = {Value List:CustomerTerm}

Rule # 349 (Not Active)
   Desc - 14.1.1 - Hold Hemolyzed Samples
   Child of Rule # 348 - Then
   If - ( {Result} {On Any Test} {NOT} = "" ) {AND} ( {Hemolyzed (PUF01)} = "Yes" ) {AND} ( {Hold Test Flag} {On That Test} {NOT} {Contains} "HEMOLYZED" )
   Then - {Set} {Hold Test Flag} {On That Test} = {Hold Test Flag} {On That Test} {Concatenated With} ",HEMOLYZED SAMPLE"

Rule # 350 (Not Active)
   Desc - 14.1.2 - Hold Lipemic Samples

   Then - {Set} {Hold Test Flag} {On That Test} = {Hold Test Flag} {On That Test} {Concatenated With} ",LIPEMIC SAMPLE"


--- Live - Incoming status - Before Message Queued Internally ---

Rule # 1
   Desc - IS.1 - Set SUIF03=DOUBLEQUERY if SUIF03=QUERY or RESULT-EXCEPTION
   If - ( {Last Query to IM Date/Time} {NOT} = "" ) {AND} ( {Specimen Action} = "Q" ) {AND} ( ( {Last Queried or Resulted} = "QUERY" ) {OR} ( {Last Queried or Resulted} = "RESULT-EXCEPTION" ) )
   Then - {Set} {Last Queried or Resulted} = "DOUBLEQUERY"

Rule # 2
   Desc - IS.2 - Set SUIF03=QUERY on Query if SUIF03=RESULT or Null
   If - ( {Last Query to IM Date/Time} {NOT} = "" ) {AND} ( {Specimen Action} = "Q" ) {AND} ( {Last Queried or Resulted} {NOT} = "QUERY" ) {AND} ( {Last Queried or Resulted} {NOT} = "DOUBLEQUERY" ) {AND} ( {Last Queried or Resulted} {NOT} = "RESULT-EXCEPTION" )
   Then - {Set} {Last Queried or Resulted} = "QUERY"
